                                <br>
                                User's primary goal is to get an answer to a certain question or find a specific piece of information from system. 
                                Conversational flow where users interact with the bot to extract information
                                from Lighthouse about tree metadata and KPI metrics.
                                Users can inquire about various aspects of Lighthouse,
                                including its modules/components such as metrics, nodes, aggregation, anomalies,
                                cohorts, and insights

                                        <tr><th class="text-left">Tree Description</th></tr>
                                        <tr><td  class="text-left"><div class="message brainspark" id="message9"><div>
    <h3 style="color:#043365">Global Travel Sales Performance</h3><hr>
    <h5 style="display: inline;color:royalblue"><b>Tree Structure :</b></h5>
        <ul><li><pre>Sales Analysis
├── Domestic
│   ├── Domestic Airline Tickets
│   └── Domestic Hotel Bookings
└── International
    ├── International Airline Tickets
    └── International Hotel Bookings
</pre></li></ul>
    <h5 style="display: inline;color:royalblue"><b>Basic Tree Info :</b></h5>
        <pre><ul><li><b>Tree ID:</b> 1</li>
<li><b>Tree Name:</b> Global Travel Sales Performance</li>
<li><b>Group:</b> Multi-Domain</li>
<li><b>Tree Objective:</b> The "Global Travel Sales Performance KPI Tree" is a hierarchical key performance 
    indicator (KPI) structure designed to provide a comprehensive overview of sales and booking 
    metrics in the travel industry. This tree is specifically tailored to the "travel_sales_dataset"
    and encompasses two primary nodes: "Domestic" and "International."</li>
</ul></pre>
    <h5 style="display: inline;color:royalblue"><b>KPI-Metrics :</b></h5>
        <ul><li><pre>Total Sale <b>(Primary KPI-Metric)</b>
Total Bookings
</pre></li></ul>
    <h5 style="display: inline;color:royalblue"><b>Tree Filters :</b></h5>
        <ul><li><pre><b>month:</b> FEB-2023, JAN-2023, DEC-2022, NOV-2022, OCT-2022, ... (+3 more)
</pre></li></ul>
    
        <h5 style="display: inline;color:royalblue"><b>Cohorts :</b></h5>
        <pre><ul><li><b>Travel-Sales-Profession</b> (Categorical):<br>Artist,<br>Doctor,<br>Engineer,<br>Entertainment,<br>Executive,<br> ... (+5 more)
</li>
<li><b>age_group</b> (Categorical):<br>Age 30-45, Age 45-60, Age &lt;30, Age &gt;60
</li>
</ul></pre></div></div></td></tr>

                            <br>
                            User's primary goal is to changes the state of the application's data or seek information from outside using OpenAI LLM Models.  
                            Conversational flow where users interact with the bot by requesting it to perform some
                            actions, such as creating a tree, generating content, provide some analysis with intelligence using
                            OpenAI's LLM models,
                            or executing tasks like cloning a tree.
